# 轻小说 2021 NPM、PYPI、DockerHub 备份

## 艾蕾GY(elegy) - 泉和良 - 20210305


### Docker

```
docker pull apachecn0/ailei-gy-elegy-quanheliang-20210305
docker run -tid -p <port>:80 apachecn0/ailei-gy-elegy-quanheliang-20210305
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### PYPI

```
pip install ailei-gy-elegy-quanheliang-20210305
ailei-gy-elegy-quanheliang-20210305 <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### NPM

```
npm install -g ailei-gy-elegy-quanheliang-erlingeryilingsanlingwu
ailei-gy-elegy-quanheliang-erlingeryilingsanlingwu <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

npm install -g zuiqiang-mofashi-de-yindun-jihua-erlingeryiyiererer
zuiqiang-mofashi-de-yindun-jihua-erlingeryiyiererer <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

## 最强奴隶商的烙印魔术与美少女的堕落 - 初美阳一 - 20210512


### Docker

```
docker pull apachecn0/zuiqiang-nuli-shang-de-luoyin-moshu-yu-meishaonv-de-duoluo-chumeiyang-yi-20210512
docker run -tid -p <port>:80 apachecn0/zuiqiang-nuli-shang-de-luoyin-moshu-yu-meishaonv-de-duoluo-chumeiyang-yi-20210512
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### PYPI

```
pip install zuiqiang-nuli-shang-de-luoyin-moshu-yu-meishaonv-de-duoluo-chumeiyang-yi-20210512
zuiqiang-nuli-shang-de-luoyin-moshu-yu-meishaonv-de-duoluo-chumeiyang-yi-20210512 <port>
# 访问 http://localhost:{port} 查看文档
```

### NPM

```
